249 \textcolor{comment}{/*  MAIN DISPATCHING ROUTINE FOR GOLOFT/PLOTFT */}
250 
251 
252 \textcolor{comment}{/*  CANONICAL FORM OF SS GEOMETRY */}
253 
254 \textcolor{comment}{/*  HELP ARRAY FOR VECTOR TRANSFORMATION */}
255 
256 \textcolor{comment}{/*   STORAGE FOR REGION SEGMENTS */}
257 
258 \textcolor{comment}{/*   ***  20.  DARRAY BLOCK  *** */}
259 
260 \textcolor{comment}{/*   PRINT BUFFER */}
261 
262 
263 
264 
265 \textcolor{comment}{/*  GOLOFT COMMON */}
266 
267 \textcolor{comment}{/*  VECTOR-COMPONENTS OF THE TOOL-AXIS-VECTOR */}
268 
269 
270 \textcolor{comment}{/* UVCONS:    U-, V- CONSTANTS, GIVEN BY "UCONST,U" OR "VCONST,V" */}
271 
272 \textcolor{comment}{/* UVA:       STARTPARAMETER GIVEN BY "START,S" */}
273 
274 \textcolor{comment}{/* UVE:       ENDPARAMETER GIVEN BY "THRU,T" */}
275 
276 \textcolor{comment}{/* TOL:       INCREMENTS BY "INCR,I", ERROR OF CHORD BY "CHORD,C" */}
277 
278 \textcolor{comment}{/* VL:        LENGTH-PARAMETER GIVEN BY "LENGTH,L" */}
279 
280 \textcolor{comment}{/* NU:        AMOUNT OF INTERMEDIATE LINES IN DIRECTION    UCONST */}
281 
282 \textcolor{comment}{/* NV:        AMOUNT OF INTERMEDIATE LINES IN DIRECTION    VCONST */}
283 
284 \textcolor{comment}{/* IART:      IART = 1   PLOTFT/SCURV,.........,PARAM,.... */}
285 \textcolor{comment}{/*            IART = 2   PLOTFT/SCURV,.........,FLOW ,.... */}
286 \textcolor{comment}{/*            IART = 3   PLOTFT/SSURF,UCONST,U,........... */}
287 \textcolor{comment}{/*            IART = 4   PLOTFT/SSURF,VCONST,V,........... */}
288 \textcolor{comment}{/*            IART = 5   PLOTFT/SSURF,GRID,............... */}
289 \textcolor{comment}{/*            IART = 6   GOLOFT/SSURF,UCONST,U,........... */}
290 \textcolor{comment}{/*            IART = 7   GOLOFT/SSURF,VCONST,V,........... */}
291 
292 \textcolor{comment}{/* INVERS:    INVERSION OF THE POINT-SEQUENCE */}
293 
294 \textcolor{comment}{/* MIRROR:    INVERSION OF THE MANUFACTURED SIDE  (DIRECTION OF NORMAL) */}
295 
296 \textcolor{comment}{/* NORMAL:   =1, IF  TLAXIS/NORMPS GIVEN; SURFACE-NORMAL = AXIS-DIRECTION */}
297 
298 \textcolor{comment}{/* INCR:     =1 IF "INCR,I", =0 IF "CHORD,C" GIVEN */}
299 
300 \textcolor{comment}{/* IAT:       IAT   = 0 AT NOT PROGRAMMED */}
301 \textcolor{comment}{/*            IAT   = 1 AT   "AT,A",        = 2 AT   "AT,TO,PL1" */}
302 \textcolor{comment}{/*            IAT   = 3 AT   "AT,ON,PL1,    = 4 AT   "AT,PAST,PL1 */}
303 
304 \textcolor{comment}{/* ISTRT:     ISTRT = 0 START NOT PROGRAMMED */}
305 \textcolor{comment}{/*            ISTRT = 1 AT   "START,A",     = 2 AT   "START,TO,PL1" */}
306 \textcolor{comment}{/*            ISTRT = 3 AT   "START,ON,PL1, = 4 AT   "START,PAST,PL1 */}
307 
308 \textcolor{comment}{/* ITHRU:     ITHRU = 0 THRU NOT PROGRAMMED */}
309 \textcolor{comment}{/*            ITHRU = 1 AT   "THRU,A",      = 2 AT   "THRU,TO,PL1" */}
310 \textcolor{comment}{/*            ITHRU = 3 AT   "THRU,ON,PL1,  = 4 AT   "THRU,PAST,PL1 */}
311 
312 \textcolor{comment}{/*   LOGIC-FUNCTION FOR CHECKING THE GEOMETRY */}
313 
314 \textcolor{comment}{/*  BLANK-COMMON */}
315 
316 \textcolor{comment}{/*  OUTPUT-ARRAY OF THE HEADER */}
317 
318 \textcolor{comment}{/*     UNLABELLED COMMON */}
319 
320 \textcolor{comment}{/* ---     SIZE OF BLANK COMMON IS ALLOCATED RIGHT HERE. */}
321 
322 
323 
324 
325 
326 
327 \textcolor{comment}{/*    THE ORIGINAL COMMON-DIMENSION-EQUIVALENCE (CDE) PACKAGE TOTAL */}
328 \textcolor{comment}{/*    HAS BEEN REPLACED BY INDIVIDUAL COMMON BLOCKS, AND EQUIVALENCE */}
329 \textcolor{comment}{/*    STATEMENTS HAVE BEEN ELIMINATED AS FAR AS POSSIBLE. */}
330 
331

333 
334 \textcolor{comment}{/*    REAL VARIABLES USED BY ARELEM, WHICH MUST REMAIN INVIOLATE */}
